###########################
# Australasia Events
###########################
# By VICTIMS
###########################

add_namespace = austral

### INTRO EVENTS ### 1-100
country_event = { #Status of the Confederation
	id = austral.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.1.t
	desc = austral.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			NZL = {
				## Send everyone to AST
				every_unit_leader = {
					add_trait = { trait = AST_new_zealander }
					set_unit_leader_flag = NZL_character
					set_nationality = AST
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = austral.2
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #1936 Australian Labor Party Leadership Election
	id = austral.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.10 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.10.t
	desc = austral.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_labor_poster

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Curtin
		name = austral.10.a
		set_country_flag = AST_curtin_party
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.11
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.12
					days = 6
				}
			}

			
		}
	}
	option = { # Forde
		name = austral.10.b 
		set_country_flag = AST_forde_party
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.11
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.12
					days = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #An Approach to the Labor Reconciliation
	id = austral.18
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.18 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.18.t
	desc = austral.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_lang_labor

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # The ALP restablishes its hold
		name = austral.18.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_slp
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_lang
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_ALP_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_ALP_strength value = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = austral.19
				days = 9
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Lang 
		name = austral.18.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_slp
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_labor
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_ALP_AS_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_ALP_AS_strength value = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = austral.19
				days = 9
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # the socialists
		name = austral.18.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_labor
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_lang
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_SLP_banned } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_SLP_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_SLP_strength value = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = austral.19
				days = 9
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = AST_election
					option = AST_path_country
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = AST_election
					option = AST_path_afal
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_nats_lead_coalition
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.27
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # the Country party's threats win primacy
		name = austral.26.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = AST_election
					option = AST_path_nationalist
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = AST_election
					option = AST_path_afal
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_nats_lead_coalition } }
		set_country_flag = AST_cnt_lead_coalition
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.27
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # The coalition is broken ahead of the election
		name = austral.26.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_nationalist
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = AST_election
						option = AST_path_country
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = AST_election
					option = AST_path_afal
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_nats_lead_coalition } }
		set_country_flag = AST_no_coalition 
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.27
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}


country_event = { #The labor partie  Stabilise Ahead of the Election
	id = austral.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.27 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.27.t
	desc = austral.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_curtin

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.27.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_ALP_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_ALP_AS_strength
			}
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_ALP_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_SLP_strength
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.30
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.101
					days = 6
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_ALP_wins
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.27.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_ALP_AS_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_ALP_strength
			}
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_ALP_AS_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_SLP_strength
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.30
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.101
					days = 6
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_ALP_AS_wins
			set_country_flag = AST_lang_party
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.27.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_SLP_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_ALP_AS_strength
			}
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_SLP_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_ALP_strength
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.30
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.101
					days = 6
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_SLP_wins
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.15 }
	}
}

			} else_if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_NZL_coalition_count
						compare = equals
						value = 2
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = AST_NZL_reform_2
			} else_if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_NZL_coalition_count
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 3
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = AST_NZL_reform_3
			}
		}
	}

	desc = { text = austral.113.d }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = austral.113.a
		set_country_flag = AST_is_federated 
		remove_power_balance = {
    		id = AST_union
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_is_federated
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_is_republic }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_federation
		}
		add_ideas = AST_is_federated_idea
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.113.b
		add_ideas = AST_unified_australasia
		trigger = {
			not = { has_country_flag = AST_is_republic }
		}
		remove_power_balance = {
    		id = AST_union
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # yes
		name = austral.160.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_arb_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_arbitration_ideas
			}
			else_if = {  limit = { has_country_flag = AST_federal_debts_referendum}
				add_ideas = AST_federalist_debts_ideas
			}
			if = {  limit = { has_country_flag = AST_commie_referendum }
				add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = -0.99 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = -0.99 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = -0.99 }
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = AST_syn_name_dc
					set_country_flag = AST_tot_name_dc
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = radical_socialist 
					long_name = AST_banned_party_long
					name = AST_banned_party
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = totalist 
					long_name = AST_banned_party_long
					name = AST_banned_party
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = syndicalist 
					long_name = AST_banned_party_long
					name = AST_banned_party
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_bank_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_bank_control_idea
			}
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_14_points_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_14_points_idea
			}
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_social_services_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_social_services_federalised_idea
			}
			if = { limit ={ has_country_flag = AST_republic_referendum }
				AST_become_republic = yes
				country_event = {
					id = austral.113
					days = 3
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = AST_arb_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_federal_debts_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_commie_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_bank_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_14_points_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_republic_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_social_services_referendum
		}
	}
	option = { # yes
		name = austral.160.b
	}
}

# Death of John Curtin
country_event = {
	id = austral.309
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.309 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.309.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_curtinspeech

	desc = {
		text = austral.309.d.hog
		trigger = {
			has_idea = AST_John_J_Curtin_hog_sde
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = austral.309.d.nothog
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = AST_John_J_Curtin_hog_sde
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		date > 1945.7.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = John_J_Curtin_dead
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.309.a
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = AST_John_Curtin_hog_sde
			}
			remove_ideas = AST_John_Curtin_hog_sde
			add_ideas = AST_Joseph_Chifley_hog_sde
			set_country_flag = AST_chifley_party
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = AST_is_republic
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Joseph Chifley"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Joseph_Chifley.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = John_J_Curtin_dead
	}
}

### THE NEW ZEALAND CRISIS ### 400-500

country_event = { # New Zealand leaves peacefully
	id = austral.400
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.400"
		remove_power_balance = {
    		id = AST_union
		}
	}
	title = { text = austral.400.t }
	desc = { text = austral.400.d }
	picture = GFX_report_event_NZL_coalition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.400.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		284 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		723 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		NZL = {
			set_country_flag = NZL_voted_to_leave
			transfer_state = 284
			transfer_state = 723
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = nzl.30
					days = 3
				}
				AST = {
					NZL = {
						transfer_technology = yes
					}
					set_nationality = {
			        target_country = NZL
			        character = NZL_Peter_Buck
			        }
				}
				load_oob = "NZL"
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_1
					amount = 1000
					producer = CAN
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = convoy_1
					amount = 25
					producer = CAN
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = AST
				}
				add_to_faction = NZL
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_trait = AST_new_zealander }
			remove_unit_leader_trait = AST_new_zealander
			set_nationality = NZL
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NZL_Sidney_Holland_hog_sco
			}
			remove_ideas = NZL_Sidney_Holland_hog_sco
		}
		set_country_flag = Sidney_G_Holland_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.401
				days = 3
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				news_event = {
					id = worldnews.132
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		NZL = {
			change_tag_from = AST
		}
		name = austral.400.b
		add_political_power = -100
		284 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		723 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		NZL = {
			set_country_flag = NZL_voted_to_leave
			transfer_state = 284
			transfer_state = 723
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = nzl.30
					days = 3
				}
				AST = {
					NZL = {
						transfer_technology = yes
					}

# Australasia loses New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.401
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.401 FROM = [From.GetName]" 
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_power_balance = {
				id = AST_union
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
			AST_update_party_names = yes
		}
	}
	title = austral.401.t
	desc = austral.401.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_newzealand

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_war = no
		NOT = { owns_state = 284 } #New Zealand
		NOT = { owns_state = 723 } #South Island
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes 

	option = {
		name = austral.401.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_is_republic OR = { has_country_flag = AST_dem_focus_move has_country_flag = AST_red_focus_move } }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_australia_republic
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT } has_country_flag = AST_whites_focus_move }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_australia_cromwell
		}
		else = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_australia
		}
		284 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
				add_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		723 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
				add_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
	}
}

# Australia regains New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.402
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.402 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.402 FROM = [From.GetName]" 
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
			AST_update_party_names = yes
		}
	}
	title = austral.402.t
	desc = austral.402.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_newzealand

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		owns_state = 284 #New Zealand
		owns_state = 723 #South Island
	}
	fire_only_once = yes 
	option = {
		name = austral.402.a
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_red_focus_move } }
			add_state_core = 284
			add_state_core = 723
			hidden_effect = {
				NZL = {
				set_nationality = {
			    target_country = AST
			    character = NZL_Peter_Buck
			    }
			    }
			}
		} 
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_red_focus_move }
			set_country_flag = AST_NZL_occupation
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AST_NZL_unity_1_idea }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AST_NZL_unity_1_idea
					add_idea = AST_NZL_forced_intergration_0
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AST_NZL_unity_2_idea }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AST_NZL_unity_2_idea
					add_idea = AST_NZL_forced_intergration_0
				}
			}
			else = { add_ideas = AST_NZL_forced_intergration_0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_is_republic has_country_flag = AST_dem_focus_move }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_republic
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT } has_country_flag = AST_whites_focus_move }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_cromwell
		}
		else = {
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_red_focus_move } 
				set_cosmetic_tag = AST_republic
			}
			else = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = AST_federation
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.402.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		284 = { remove_claim_by = AST }
		723 = { remove_claim_by = AST }
		AST = {
			remove_state_core = 284
			remove_state_core = 723
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			NZL = { NZL_become_republic = yes }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NZL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		
		AST = {
			set_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
		}
	}
}

# The war begins with New Zealand
country_event = {

	title = austral.404.t
	desc = austral.404.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_army1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		284 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = NZL } #New Zealand
		723 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = NZL } #South Island
		OR = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		NZL = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.404.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = NZL
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NZL = {
				set_country_flag = NZL_war_of_succsession
				country_event = { id = nzl.1 days = 1 } #start the war
			} 
			country_event = { id = nzl.501 days = 125 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.404.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		NZL = { 
			set_country_flag = NZL_war_of_succsession
			country_event = {
				id = nzl.19
				days = 3
			} 
		}
	}
}

# Peace deal - AST has captured New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.405
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.405 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.405.t
	desc = austral.405.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ast_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_war_with = NZL
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		controls_state = 284 #New Zealand
		controls_state = 723 #South Island
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.405.a # It is time to call for a truce
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 150
			ENT = { remove_from_faction = NZL }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 523 #New Guinea
						state = 636 #Fiji
					}
					OR = {
						is_controlled_by = ENT
						controller = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = AST }
					remove_core_of = AST
					add_claim_by = AST
				}
				ENT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.405.b # No! We will continue this war until it is finished!
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
	}
}

	title = austral.500.t
	desc = austral.500.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.500.a #Yes - Australasia is our friend
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				AST = {
					has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_accepted_trade
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ENT }
			add_political_power = 75
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		AST = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = AST_trade_deal
			}
			country_event = { id = austral.501 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.500.b #No, we can't be bothered with this
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					tag = ENT
					tag = USA
					tag = CAL
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		AST = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = AST_trade_deal_refused
			}
			country_event = { id = austral.502 days = 7 }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_guaranteed = GEA }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = GEA
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #maintain mainland descrtimiation
		name = austral.520.e
		trigger = {has_country_flag = AST_Germ_peace has_country_flag = AST_Jap_peace }
		clr_country_flag = AST_Jap_peace
		clr_country_flag = AST_Germ_peace
		if = { limit = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = GEA }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = GEA
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_guaranteed = JAP }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = JAP
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_guaranteed = GEA }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = GEA
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = JAP }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = JAP
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = austral.525.d

		name = austral.525.a #We have no choice - let them have the land
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				is_subject_of = AST
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AST
			modifier = KR_returned_land
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				not = { is_subject_of = AST }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = AST
						not = { is_core_of = PREV }
					}
					AST = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		} else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = AST
					}
					AST = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		AST = { country_event = austral.3368 }
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.525.b #What? No! They will have to fight for it
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_subject_of = AST
			}
		}
		AST = { country_event = austral.3369 }
		add_political_power = 50
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AST modifier = KR_outraged }
	}
}

	title = austral.535.t
	desc = austral.535.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral

	fire_only_once = yes

		tag = AST

			has_country_flag = Joseph_A_Lyons_dead
		}
	}

		name = austral.535.a
		set_country_flag = Joseph_A_Lyons_dead
		add_political_power = -10
	}
}

	id = austral.800
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.800 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	desc = austral.800.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_country_party

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #  Saturn devours jupitar
		name = austral.800.a
		set_country_flag = AST_country_paty_absorbs_nats
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand }
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = market_liberal 
				long_name = AST_australia_social_conservative_party_long
				name = AST_australia_social_conservative_party
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = market_liberal 
				long_name = AST_social_conservative_party_long
				name = AST_social_conservative_party
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #  Saturn devours jupitar but change name to lib national
		name = austral.800.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AST_country_paty_absorbs_nats
			set_country_flag = AST_ml_name_dc
			set_country_flag = AST_sc_name_dc
		}
		set_party_name = { 
    		ideology = market_liberal 
    		long_name = AST_lib_nat_party_long
   		 	name = AST_lib_nat_party
		}
		set_party_name = { 
    		ideology = social_conservative 
    		long_name = AST_lib_nat_party_long
   		 	name = AST_lib_nat_party
		}
	}
	option = { #  Saturn devours jupitar but change to country nat
		name = austral.800.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AST_country_paty_absorbs_nats
			set_country_flag = AST_ml_name_dc
			set_country_flag = AST_sc_name_dc
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		set_party_name = { 
    		ideology = market_liberal 
    		long_name = AST_country_nat_party_long
   		 	name = AST_country_nat_party
		}
		set_party_name = { 
    		ideology = social_conservative 
    		long_name = AST_country_nat_party_long
   		 	name = AST_country_nat_party
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.800.e
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_NZL_savage_death

	trigger= {
		owns_state = 284
		owns_state = 723
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.905.a
		set_country_flag = AST_NZL_occupation
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = AST_NZL_unity_1_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = AST_NZL_unity_1_idea
				add_idea = AST_NZL_forced_intergration_0
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = AST_NZL_unity_2_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = AST_NZL_unity_2_idea
				add_idea = AST_NZL_forced_intergration_0
			}
		}
		else = { add_ideas = AST_NZL_forced_intergration_0 }
		remove_state_core = 723
		remove_state_core = 284
		add_state_claim = 723
		add_state_claim = 284
		set_country_flag = AST_is_federated
		set_cosmetic_tag = AST_federation
	}
	option = { # free
		name = austral.905.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		country_event = {
			id = austral.400 days = 5
		}
	}
}

		}

		add_ideas = AST_Rex_Ingamells_hog_pau

		}

		}

	}

					is_core_of = AST

					is_controlled_by = AST
				}
				save_event_target_as = attack_state

		}

		event_target:attack_state = {

			}
		}
	}

	desc = austral.3366.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_de_leon

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.3366.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = 75
		add_stability = 0.0075
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CSA }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CSA
				modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.3366.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { country_exists = CSA }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit  = { has_country_flag = AST_iww_elected }
				set_cosmetic_tag = AST_obu_iww
			} else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = AST_obu_slp
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = USA }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = USA
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = NEE }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = NEE
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = COR }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = COR
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = BBR }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = BBR
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}	
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = TXS }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = TXS
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}	
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = TEX }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = TEX
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}	
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = WCC }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = WCC
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = CAL }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = CAL
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}
		create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = ALA }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ALA
			}
			add_claim_by = AST
		}
	}
}
